[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction#content-area)

Get Started

Introduction

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

On this page

*   [Start Building](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction#start-building)
    

Etherscan is the leading blockchain explorer, search, API, and analytics platform for Ethereum and other EVM-compatible chains. With Etherscan API V2, we‚Äôve unified all 60+ [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
 under a single account and API key system. Your app becomes multichain üåà simply by updating the `chainid` parameter to support BNB Smart Chain (BSC), Base, Arbitrum, HyperEVM, and more.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction#start-building)

Start Building
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Get Stablecoin Transfers to an Address\
--------------------------------------\
\
Check for USDC/USDT/PYUSD token transfers to an address.\
\
Token Transfers Endpoint](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokentx)
[Get Top Token Holders\
---------------------\
\
Analyze the largest holders of YieldBasis(Ethereum), Aster(BNB) and other newly launched tokens.\
\
Top Holders Endpoint](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/toptokenholders)
[Get Address Portfolio\
---------------------\
\
List all token balances for an address, across chains.\
\
Address Portfolio Endpoint](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokenbalance)
[Get Address Name Tag\
--------------------\
\
Get name tags and labels associated with an address, such as exchange deposits ‚ÄúCoinbase 10‚Äù.\
\
Name Tag Endpoint](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getaddresstag)

[Getting an API Key](https://docs.etherscan.io/getting-an-api-key)

Get Address ERC20 Token Holding

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

GET

/

v2

/

api

Try it

Copy

Ask AI

curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=account&action=addresstokenbalance&address=0x983e3660c0bE01991785F80f266A84B911ab59b0&page=1&offset=100&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "TokenAddress": "0xffffffff2ba8f66d4e51811c5190992176930278",\
          "TokenName": "Furucombo",\
          "TokenSymbol": "COMBO",\
          "TokenQuantity": "1861606940000000000",\
          "TokenDivisor": "18",\
          "TokenPriceUSD": "0.000891470000000000"\
        },\
        {\
          "TokenAddress": "0x53a1e9912323b8016424d6287286e3b6de263f76",\
          "TokenName": "PUTIN Token",\
          "TokenSymbol": "PTT",\

      ]
    }

This is a PRO endpoint, available to any [paid tier](https://etherscan.io/apis)

This [historical endpoint](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/rate-limits)
 is throttled to 2 calls/s

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokenbalance#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokenbalance#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokenbalance#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokenbalance#param-module)

module

string

default:"account"

Set to `account` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokenbalance#param-action)

action

string

default:"addresstokenbalance"

Set to `addresstokenbalance` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokenbalance#param-address)

address

string

default:"0x983e3660c0bE01991785F80f266A84B911ab59b0"

Address to check for token holdings.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokenbalance#param-page)

page

integer

default:"1"

Page number for pagination.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokenbalance#param-offset)

offset

integer

default:"100"

Number of records per page.

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=account&action=addresstokenbalance&address=0x983e3660c0bE01991785F80f266A84B911ab59b0&page=1&offset=100&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"
    

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "TokenAddress": "0xffffffff2ba8f66d4e51811c5190992176930278",\
          "TokenName": "Furucombo",\
          "TokenSymbol": "COMBO",\
          "TokenQuantity": "1861606940000000000",\
          "TokenDivisor": "18",\
          "TokenPriceUSD": "0.000891470000000000"\
        },\
        {\
          "TokenAddress": "0x53a1e9912323b8016424d6287286e3b6de263f76",\

 is throttled to 2 calls/s

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftbalance#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftbalance#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftbalance#param-module)

module

string

default:"account"

Set to `account` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftbalance#param-action)

action

string

default:"addresstokennftbalance"

Set to `addresstokennftbalance` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftbalance#param-address)

address

string

default:"0x6b52e83941eb10f9c613c395a834457559a80114"

Address to check for NFT holdings.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftbalance#param-page)

page

integer

default:"1"

Page number for pagination.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftbalance#param-offset)

offset

integer

default:"100"

Number of records per page.

/

v1

/

api.ashx

Try it

Export Address Tags

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api-metadata.etherscan.io/v1/api.ashx

Response

Copy

Ask AI

"address";"nametag";"internal_nametag";"url";"shortdescription";"notes_1";"notes_2";"labels";"labels_slug";"reputation";"other_attributes";"lastupdatedtimestamp"

    "0x00000000006a2b6820feb8d5ac00cb6800795d8f";"Fake_Phishing326507";"";"";"";"There are reports that this address was used in a Phishing scam. Please exercise caution when interacting with it.";"";"Phish / Hack";"phish-hack";"2";"";"1711418316"
    "0x0000000000d67e5d5f991a40f04ed40fa3b150df";"Fake_Phishing326508";"";"";"";"There are reports that this address was used in a Phishing scam. Please exercise caution when interacting with it.";"";"Phish / Hack";"phish-hack";"2";"";"1711418362"
    "0x0000000000e7f7e18e6b7890ea1227ff088e6653";"Fake_Phishing686515";"";"";"";"There are reports that this address was used in a Phishing scam. Please exercise caution when interacting with it. Reported by ScamSniffer.";"";"Phish / Hack";"phish-hack";"2";"";"1734599538"
    "0x00000000020e203eb8fc5d0724e7c93e6b002c71";"Fake_Phishing119146";"";"";"";"Warning! This address may be attempting to impersonate a similar looking address. Please proceed with caution.";"";"Phish / Hack";"phish-hack";"2";"";"1738570688"

This is a PRO endpoint, available to the [Enterprise tier](https://etherscan.io/apis)

This endpoint is throttled to 2 calls/s and 100 calls/day

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/exportaddresstags#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/exportaddresstags#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/exportaddresstags#param-module)

module

string

default:"nametag"

Set to `nametag` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/exportaddresstags#param-action)

action

string

default:"exportaddresstags"

Set to `exportaddresstags` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/exportaddresstags#param-label)

label

string

default:"ofac-sanctioned"

Use the [Label Master List](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlabelmasterlist)
 to discover categeories like `phish-hack`, or pass `all` to export every label.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/exportaddresstags#param-format)

format

string

default:"csv"

The response format, currently only in `.csv`.

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    "address";"nametag";"internal_nametag";"url";"shortdescription";"notes_1";"notes_2";"labels";"labels_slug";"reputation";"other_attributes";"lastupdatedtimestamp"
    "0x0000000000000000000000000000000000001111";"Fake_Phishing589039";"";"";"";"There are reports that this address was used in a Phishing scam. Please exercise caution when interacting with it. Reported by HashDit.";"";"Phish / Hack";"phish-hack";"2";"";"1728292621"

# Introduction - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Get Started

Introduction

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

On this page

*   [Etherscan MCP Server](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction#etherscan-mcp-server)
    

Etherscan‚Äôs MCP [(Model Context Protocol)](https://modelcontextprotocol.io/)
 allows you to connect Etherscan and [60+ supported chain](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
 data to your AI models such as ChatGPT, Claude. An ELI5, the MCP standard provides a list of tools that your model can call to lookup information via the Etherscan API. Yes, it is an API wrapper. This avoids common problem of LLMs making things up (hallucination) or getting blocked by captcha on a web search. Some use cases of our beta users

*   Comparing Solidity code with actual contracts deployed on chain
*   Customer support for bridge transactions, if the transactions has arrived
*   Portfolio management agents

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction#etherscan-mcp-server)

Etherscan MCP Server
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We host a Streamable HTTP MCP server at

Copy

Ask AI

    https://mcp.etherscan.io/mcp
    

You will need to authenticate using your Etherscan API key, as a bearer token in the header like

Copy

Ask AI

    Authorization: Bearer YourEtherscanApiKey
    

‚åòI

---

# Get Daily Average Block Size - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgblocksize#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Navigation

Blocks

Get Daily Average Block Size

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

GET

/

v2

/

api

Try it

Copy

Ask AI

curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=stats&action=dailyavgblocksize&startdate=2019-02-01&enddate=2019-02-28&sort=desc&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-01",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1548979200",\
          "blockSize_bytes": 20373\
        },\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-02",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1549065600",\
          "blockSize_bytes": 17499\
        }\
      ]
    }

This is a PRO endpoint, available to any [paid tier](https://etherscan.io/apis)

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgblocksize#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgblocksize#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgblocksize#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID you query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgblocksize#param-module)

module

string

default:"stats"

Set to `stats` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgblocksize#param-action)

action

string

default:"dailyavgblocksize"

Set to `dailyavgblocksize` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgblocksize#param-startdate)

startdate

string

default:"2019-02-01"

Starting date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgblocksize#param-enddate)

enddate

string

default:"2019-02-28"

Ending date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgblocksize#param-sort)

sort

string

default:"desc"

Sort order, either `asc` or `desc`.

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=stats&action=dailyavgblocksize&startdate=2019-02-01&enddate=2019-02-28&sort=desc&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"
    

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-01",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1548979200",\
          "blockSize_bytes": 20373\
        },\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-02",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1549065600",\
          "blockSize_bytes": 17499\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

[Get Block Number by Timestamp](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getblocknobytime)
[Get Daily Block Count and Rewards](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyblkcount)

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlabelmasterlist#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlabelmasterlist#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlabelmasterlist#param-module)

module

string

default:"nametag"

Set to `nametag` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlabelmasterlist#param-action)

action

string

default:"getlabelmasterlist"

Set to `getlabelmasterlist` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlabelmasterlist#param-format)

format

string

default:"zip"

The format of the response. Can be either `zip` or `csv`. Note that the labels `binance`, `deposit-address`, and `all` must use `zip` format.

# Get Native Balance for an Address - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balance#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Account

Get Native Balance for an Address

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

GET

/

v2

/

api

Try it

Get Native Balance for an Address

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
       "status":"1",
       "message":"OK",
       "result":"172774397764084972158218"
    }

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balance#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balance#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balance#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balance#param-module)

module

string

default:"account"

Set to `account` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balance#param-action)

action

string

default:"balance"

Set to `balance` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balance#param-address)

address

string

default:"0xde0b295669a9fd93d5f28d9ec85e40f4cb697bae"

The address to query, like `0xfefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefe`. Up to 20 addresses can be queried, separated by commas.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balance#param-tag)

tag

string

default:"latest"

Use `latest` for the last block number of the chain. Also accepts a specific block number in hex format, like `0x10d4f` up to the last 128 blocks. For historical balances, use the [Historical Balance](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balancehistory)
 endpoint.

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
       "status":"1",
       "message":"OK",
       "result":"172774397764084972158218"
    }
    

[V2 Migration](https://docs.etherscan.io/v2-migration)
[Get Historical Native Balance for an Address](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balancehistory)

‚åòI

# Get Historical Native Balance for an Address - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balancehistory#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Navigation

Account

Get Historical Native Balance for an Address

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

GET

/

v2

/

api

Try it

Get Historical Native Balance for an Address

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": "610538078574759898951277"
    }

This is a PRO endpoint, available to any [paid tier](https://etherscan.io/apis)

This [historical endpoint](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/rate-limits)
 is throttled to 2 calls/s

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balancehistory#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balancehistory#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balancehistory#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balancehistory#param-module)

module

string

default:"account"

Set to `account` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balancehistory#param-action)

action

string

default:"balancehistory"

Set to `balancehistory` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balancehistory#param-address)

address

string

default:"0xde0b295669a9fd93d5f28d9ec85e40f4cb697bae"

The address to query, like `0xfefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefe`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balancehistory#param-blockno)

blockno

integer

default:"8000000"

Block number to check balance at, all the way up to the genesis block `0`.

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": "610538078574759898951277"
    }
    

[Get Native Balance for an Address](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balance)
[Get Normal Transactions By Address](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/txlist)

Navigation

Resources

Reputation Reference

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

| Score | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 0   | ‚ÄôUNKNOWN‚Äô (default) |
| 1   | ‚ÄôOK‚Äô An OK reputation is not an endorsement but likely a known/public entity. |
| 2   | ‚ÄôCAUTION‚Äô Moderate Caution Advised when interacting with the address. |
| 3   | ‚ÄôUNSAFE‚Äô Extreme caution advised when interacting with the address. |

Get Started

Introduction

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

The Metadata CSV export is an Enterprise feature that allows dataset exports of [labels](https://etherscan.io/labelcloud/)
, name tags, and other metadata related to an address. This export currently supports Ethereum only, with other chains to follow. [Contact us](https://docs.etherscan.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#f293829b818782829d8086b297869a97808191939cdc9b9d)
 to for more info and to book a demo.

[Get Label Master List](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlabelmasterlist)

# Get Address ERC721 Token Inventory by Contract - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftinventory#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Tokens

Get Address ERC721 Token Inventory by Contract

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

GET

/

v2

/

api

Try it

Copy

Ask AI

curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=account&action=addresstokennftinventory&address=0x123432244443b54409430979df8333f9308a6040&contractaddress=0xed5af388653567af2f388e6224dc7c4b3241c544&page=1&offset=100&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "TokenAddress": "0xed5af388653567af2f388e6224dc7c4b3241c544",\
          "TokenId": "453"\
        },\
        {\
          "TokenAddress": "0xed5af388653567af2f388e6224dc7c4b3241c544",\
          "TokenId": "8160"\
        }\
      ]
    }

This is a PRO endpoint, available to any [paid tier](https://etherscan.io/apis)

This [historical endpoint](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/rate-limits)
 is throttled to 2 calls/s

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftinventory#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftinventory#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftinventory#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftinventory#param-module)

module

string

default:"account"

Set to `account` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftinventory#param-action)

action

string

default:"addresstokennftinventory"

Set to `addresstokennftinventory` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftinventory#param-address)

address

string

default:"0x123432244443b54409430979df8333f9308a6040"

Address to check for inventory.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftinventory#param-contractaddress)

contractaddress

string

default:"0xed5af388653567af2f388e6224dc7c4b3241c544"

ERC-721 token contract address to filter by.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftinventory#param-page)

page

integer

default:"1"

Page number for pagination.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftinventory#param-offset)

offset

integer

default:"100"

Number of records per page. Limited to 1000 records per query; use the `page` parameter for subsequent records.

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=account&action=addresstokennftinventory&address=0x123432244443b54409430979df8333f9308a6040&contractaddress=0xed5af388653567af2f388e6224dc7c4b3241c544&page=1&offset=100&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"
    

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "TokenAddress": "0xed5af388653567af2f388e6224dc7c4b3241c544",\
          "TokenId": "453"\
        },\
        {\
          "TokenAddress": "0xed5af388653567af2f388e6224dc7c4b3241c544",\
          "TokenId": "8160"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

[Get Address ERC721 Token Holding](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftbalance)
[Get Plasma Deposits by Address](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/txnbridge)

‚åòI

# Check Proxy Contract Verification Status - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/checkproxyverification#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Contracts

Check Proxy Contract Verification Status

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

GET

/

v2

/

api

Try it

Check Proxy Contract Verification Status

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "status": "0",
      "message": "NOTOK",
      "result": "The proxy contract at 0xcbdcd3815b5f975e1a2c944a9b2cd1c985a1cb7f does not seem to be verified. Please verify and publish the contract source before proceeding with this proxy verification."
    }

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/checkproxyverification#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/checkproxyverification#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/checkproxyverification#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/checkproxyverification#param-module)

module

string

default:"contract"

Set to `contract` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/checkproxyverification#param-action)

action

string

default:"checkproxyverification"

Set to `checkproxyverification` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/checkproxyverification#param-guid)

guid

string

The GUID received from the proxy verification request.

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "0",
      "message": "NOTOK",
      "result": "The proxy contract at 0xcbdcd3815b5f975e1a2c944a9b2cd1c985a1cb7f does not seem to be verified. Please verify and publish the contract source before proceeding with this proxy verification."
    }
    

[Verify Proxy Contract](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifyproxycontract)
[Get Estimation of Confirmation Time](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/gasestimate)

# Other Attributes Reference - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/other-attributes-reference#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Resources

Other Attributes Reference

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

| Header | Description |
| --- | --- |
| TT  | Token Type. Types: `erc-20` and `nft`. |
| TR  | Token Reputation. Types: `Ok`, `Poor`, `Unsafe`, `Suspicious`, `Spam`, and `BrandInfringement`. |
| SC  | Verified Smart Contract. |
| CN  | Contract Name. |
| ENS | Ethereum Name Service. |

[Reputation Reference](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/reputation-reference)

‚åòI

# Get Daily Average Gas Limit - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavggaslimit#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

Navigation

Gas Tracker

Get Daily Average Gas Limit

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

GET

/

v2

/

api

Try it

Copy

Ask AI

curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=stats&action=dailyavggaslimit&startdate=2019-02-01&enddate=2019-02-28&sort=desc&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-01",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1548979200",\
          "gasLimit": "8001360"\
        },\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-02",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1549065600",\
          "gasLimit": "8001269"\
        }\
      ]
    }

This is a PRO endpoint, available to any [paid tier](https://etherscan.io/apis)

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavggaslimit#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavggaslimit#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavggaslimit#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavggaslimit#param-module)

module

string

default:"stats"

Set to `stats` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavggaslimit#param-action)

action

string

default:"dailyavggaslimit"

Set to `dailyavggaslimit` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavggaslimit#param-startdate)

startdate

string

default:"2019-02-01"

Starting date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavggaslimit#param-enddate)

enddate

string

default:"2019-02-28"

Ending date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavggaslimit#param-sort)

sort

string

default:"desc"

Sort order either `desc` for the latest results first or `asc` for the oldest results first.

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=stats&action=dailyavggaslimit&startdate=2019-02-01&enddate=2019-02-28&sort=desc&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"
    

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-01",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1548979200",\
          "gasLimit": "8001360"\
        },\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-02",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1549065600",\
          "gasLimit": "8001269"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

[Get Gas Oracle](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/gasoracle)

api

Copy

Ask AI

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-01",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1548979200",\
          "blockTime_sec": "17.67"\
        },\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-02",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1549065600",\
          "blockTime_sec": "17.41"\

.

Starting date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgblocktime#param-enddate)

enddate

string

default:"2019-02-28"

Ending date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

string

default:"desc"

Sort order, either `asc` or `desc`.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavggasprice#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavggasprice#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavggasprice#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

startdate

default:"2019-02-01"

enddate

string

default:"2019-02-28"

Ending date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

sort

string

default:"desc"

Sort order either `desc` for the latest results first or `asc` for the oldest results first.

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Navigation

Nametags

Get Nametag (Metadata) for an Address

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

GET

/

v2

/

api

Try it

Get Nametag for an Address

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
       "status":"1",
       "message":"OK",
       "result":[\
          {\
             "address":"0xa9d1e08c7793af67e9d92fe308d5697fb81d3e43",\
             "nametag":"Coinbase 10",\
             "internal_nametag":"",\
             "url":"https://coinbase.com",\
             "shortdescription":"",\
             "notes_1":"",\
             "notes_2":"",\
             "labels":[\
                "Coinbase",\
                "Exchange"\
             ],\
             "labels_slug":[\
                "coinbase",\
                "exchange"\
             ],\
             "reputation":0,\
             "other_attributes":[\
                \
             ],\
             "lastupdatedtimestamp":1721899658\
          }\
       ]
    }

This is a PRO endpoint, available to the [Pro Plus tier](https://etherscan.io/apis)

This [historical endpoint](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/rate-limits)
 is throttled to 2 calls/s

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getaddresstag#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getaddresstag#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getaddresstag#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getaddresstag#param-module)

module

string

default:"nametag"

Set to `nametag` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getaddresstag#param-action)

action

string

default:"getaddresstag"

Set to `getaddresstag` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getaddresstag#param-address)

address

string

default:"0x0000db5C8B030AE20308AC975898E09741E70000"

The address to query, like `0x0000db5C8B030AE20308AC975898E09741E70000`.

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
       "status":"1",
       "message":"OK",
       "result":[\
          {\
             "address":"0xa9d1e08c7793af67e9d92fe308d5697fb81d3e43",\
             "nametag":"Coinbase 10",\
             "internal_nametag":"",\
             "url":"https://coinbase.com",\
             "shortdescription":"",\
             "notes_1":"",\
             "notes_2":"",\
             "labels":[\
                "Coinbase",\
                "Exchange"\
             ],\
             "labels_slug":[\
                "coinbase",\
                "exchange"\
             ],\
             "reputation":0,\
             "other_attributes":[\
                \
             ],\
             "lastupdatedtimestamp":1721899658\
          }\
       ]
    }
    

[Get Withdrawal Transactions by Address](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getwithdrawaltxs)
[Chainlist](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/chainlist)

api

Try it

Copy

Ask AI

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": {
        "LastBlock": "23467872",
        "SafeGasPrice": "0.496839934",
        "ProposeGasPrice": "0.496840168",
        "FastGasPrice": "0.55411917",
        "suggestBaseFee": "0.496839934",
        "gasUsedRatio": "0.405942555555556,0.784013777777778,0.502624148542588,0.719479644444444,0.45673524947105"
      }
    }

# Verify with Remix - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-remix#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Contract Verification

Verify with Remix

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

On this page

*   [Activate](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-remix#activate)
    
*   [Add an API Key](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-remix#add-an-api-key)
    
*   [Verify](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-remix#verify)
    

[**Remix**](https://remix.ethereum.org/)
 is a no-frills, just works in your browser Solidity development tool.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-remix#activate)

Activate
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you‚Äôve written and deployed your contract, click on the **Plugin Manager** and select **Contract Verification**. ![Remix homepage](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/T1KjV-_fSmvoQ9iv/images/remix.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=T1KjV-_fSmvoQ9iv&q=85&s=3fc42f11016731a64178367bf92964ef)

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-remix#add-an-api-key)

Add an API Key
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Etherscan verification plugin requires an API key because grumpy bots yell at us on a daily basis. Click the ‚ÄúEnable‚Äù link and add your key, leave the rest as default. ![Remix add key](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/T1KjV-_fSmvoQ9iv/images/remix-add-key.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=T1KjV-_fSmvoQ9iv&q=85&s=cdae9fb3610e98a915375504f21daf6a)

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-remix#verify)

Verify
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fill in the chain, contract address, and contract name that you deployed. Now that the Etherscan checkbox is enabled, click Verify. Without this, the contract won‚Äôt show as verified on Etherscan‚Äôs explorer. ![Remix verify](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/T1KjV-_fSmvoQ9iv/images/remix-verify.avif?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=T1KjV-_fSmvoQ9iv&q=85&s=b644174694c9aeae0bd7d25c87b453d0) Once verified, you will see a happy green ‚úÖ. ![Remix verified](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/T1KjV-_fSmvoQ9iv/images/remix-verified.avif?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=T1KjV-_fSmvoQ9iv&q=85&s=dcfc0914ab9dacc0e07ee2a734e73144)

> _This open source integration was shipped by_ [**@manuelwedler**](https://github.com/manuelwedler)
>  _and the Remix team_.

[Verify with Hardhat](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat)
[Common Verification Errors](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors)

‚åòI

Navigation

Stats

Get Daily Average Network Difficulty

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

GET

/

v2

/

api

Try it

Copy

Ask AI

curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=stats&action=dailyavgnetdifficulty&startdate=2019-02-01&enddate=2019-02-28&sort=desc&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-01",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1548979200",\
          "networkDifficulty": "2,408.028"\
        },\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-02",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1549065600",\
          "networkDifficulty": "2,358.910"\
        }\
      ]
    }

This is a PRO endpoint, available to any [paid tier](https://etherscan.io/apis)

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgnetdifficulty#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgnetdifficulty#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgnetdifficulty#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgnetdifficulty#param-module)

module

string

default:"stats"

Set to `stats` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgnetdifficulty#param-action)

action

string

default:"dailyavgnetdifficulty"

Set to `dailyavgnetdifficulty` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgnetdifficulty#param-startdate)

startdate

string

default:"2019-02-01"

Starting date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgnetdifficulty#param-enddate)

enddate

string

default:"2019-02-28"

Ending date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgnetdifficulty#param-sort)

sort

string

default:"desc"

Sort order either `desc` for the latest results first or `asc` for the oldest results first.

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=stats&action=dailyavgnetdifficulty&startdate=2019-02-01&enddate=2019-02-28&sort=desc&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"
    

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-01",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1548979200",\
          "networkDifficulty": "2,408.028"\
        },\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-02",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1549065600",\
          "networkDifficulty": "2,358.910"\
        }\
      ]
    }

# Rate Limits - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/rate-limits#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Get Started

Rate Limits

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

Historical endpoints have a rate limit of **2 calls/s** regardless of API PRO tier.

| API Tier | Rate Limit | API PRO |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Free | 3 calls/second, up to 100,000 calls/day, [selected chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)<br> only | Not Available |
| Lite | 5 calls/second, up to 100,000 calls/day | Not Available |
| Standard | 10 calls/second, up to 200,000 calls/day | Available |
| Advanced | 20 calls/second, up to 500,000 calls/day | Available |
| Professional | 30 calls/second, up to 1,000,000 calls/day | Available |
| Pro Plus | 30 calls/second, up to 1,500,000 calls/day | Available |
| Dedicated/Custom | [**Contact Us**](https://docs.etherscan.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#5332233a202623233c21271336273b36212030323d7d3a3c) | Available |

[Supported Chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
[V2 Migration](https://docs.etherscan.io/v2-migration)

‚åòI

# Common Error Messages - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Resources

Common Error Messages

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

On this page

*   [Missing or Unsupported Chain](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#missing-or-unsupported-chain)
    
*   [Invalid API Key](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#invalid-api-key)
    
*   [Max rate limit](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#max-rate-limit)
    
*   [Missing or invalid action](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#missing-or-invalid-action)
    
*   [Endpoint-specific errors](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#endpoint-specific-errors)
    
*   [Query Timeout](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#query-timeout)
    
*   [Free Tier Access](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#free-tier-access)
    

An API call that encounters an error will return 0 as its `status code` and display the cause of the error under the `result` field.

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "0",
      "message": "NOTOK",
      "result": "Max rate limit reached, please use API Key for higher rate limit"
    }
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#missing-or-unsupported-chain)

Missing or Unsupported Chain

‚ÄúMissing or unsupported chainid parameter (required for v2 api), please see chainlist for the list of supported chainids‚Äù

The chain you‚Äôve specified is not supported by us yet. It could also be that you‚Äôve sent multiple chains at the same time like `420,10`, you can only send **one** at a time.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#invalid-api-key)

Invalid API Key

‚ÄúInvalid API Key‚Äù

This error occurs when you specify an invalid API Key. Ensure you are using your **Etherscan API Key**, keys from other chains like Polygonscan/Arbiscan are not valid for V2. Keys do take a few minutes to activate, anything longer than should be alarming.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#max-rate-limit)

Max rate limit

‚ÄúMax rate limit reached, please use API Key for higher rate limit‚Äù

This error occurs when you **exceed the rate limit** assigned to your specific API key. To resolve, adhere to the [rate limits](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/rate-limits)
 of your available plan. If you are using a script or application, **apply throttling** like a token bucket to limit the frequency of calls.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#missing-or-invalid-action)

Missing or invalid action

‚ÄúError! Missing Or invalid Action name‚Äù

This error occurs when you **do not specify**, or specify an **invalid** `module` and `action` name. To resolve, **double check** your API query to use a valid module and action name. If you require some help getting started, try copying the sample queries provided in the API Playground and pasting them into your browser.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#endpoint-specific-errors)

Endpoint-specific errors

‚ÄúError! Block number already pass‚Äù‚ÄúError! Invalid address format‚Äù‚ÄúContract source code not verified‚Äù

These error messages returned are specific to certain endpoints and their **related parameters.** To resolve, kindly refer to the specific endpoint‚Äôs documentation, and check for the **correct format** or **values** to be specified as **parameters.**

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#query-timeout)

Query Timeout

‚ÄúQuery Timeout occured. Please select a smaller result dataset‚Äù‚ÄúUnexpected err, timeout occurred or server too busy. Please try again later‚Äù

This error occurs when you have sent a particularly large query that did not manage to be completed in time. To resolve, consider selecting a smaller date/block range, though you may [**ping us**](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/contact-us)
 if you think the issue may be performance related.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages#free-tier-access)

Free Tier Access

‚ÄúFree API access is not supported for this chain. Please upgrade your api plan for full chain coverage.‚Äù

Certain chains are not included under the Free tier. To access all [**supported networks**](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
, you may upgrade to any of our [**paid plans**](https://etherscan.io/apis)
, check out the affordable Lite tier.

[PRO Endpoints](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/pro-endpoints)
[Contact Us](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/contact-us)

‚åòI

---

# Common Verification Errors - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Contract Verification

Common Verification Errors

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

On this page

*   [Contract Doesn‚Äôt Match](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#contract-doesn%E2%80%99t-match)
    
*   [Solidity Compilation Error](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#solidity-compilation-error)
    
*   [Contract Not Deployed](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#contract-not-deployed)
    
*   [Missing or Invalid Library Names](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#missing-or-invalid-library-names)
    
*   [Missing Contract Name](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#missing-contract-name)
    
*   [Missing/Invalid Constructor Arguments](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#missing/invalid-constructor-arguments)
    
*   [Mismatched bytecode metadata hash](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#mismatched-bytecode-metadata-hash)
    
*   [Similar Match Found](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#similar-match-found)
    
*   [Unsupported Solc Version](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#unsupported-solc-version)
    
*   [Source Code Already Verified](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#source-code-already-verified)
    
*   [Unsupported File Import Callback](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#unsupported-file-import-callback)
    
*   [Temporary Error](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#temporary-error)
    

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#contract-doesn%E2%80%99t-match)

Contract Doesn‚Äôt Match

‚ÄúCompiled contract deployment bytecode does NOT match the transaction deployment bytecode‚Äù

The submitted source code does not match the contract code deployed on chain. Common causes include using a different compiler version or enabling optimisation runs. For an exact match to be found, both **source code** and **compiler settings** specified have to exactly match the deployment conditions, for the same bytecode to be reproduced.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#solidity-compilation-error)

Solidity Compilation Error

‚ÄúSolidity Compilation Error: Identifier not found or not unique‚Äù

A compilation issue occured due to syntax errors in your Solidity source code. Consider debugging your contract with any compiler such as [**Remix**](https://remix.ethereum.org/)
 or [**Hardhat**](https://hardhat.org/)
 and reference the error from Solidity‚Äôs [**official documentation**](https://docs.soliditylang.org/)
.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#contract-not-deployed)

Contract Not Deployed

‚ÄúUnable to locate ContractCode at 0x539a277b12a3f6723f4c1769edb11b0be7c214da‚Äù

The contract has not been deployed at the specific address at the specific chain. Check the contract address you‚Äôve deployed, if your contract deployment transaction has succeeded or if the [**chainId**](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
 specified is correct. We usually pick up deployments within a few blocks from the chaintip, this will be delayed if the chain is having high activity. But no more than a few mins, [**ping us**](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/contact-us)
 if you‚Äôve verified the contract is deployed with the Etherscan link.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#missing-or-invalid-library-names)

Missing or Invalid Library Names

‚ÄúLibrary was required but suitable match not found‚Äù

A [**library**](https://solidity-by-example.org/library/)
 was used in your contract deployment, but was not specified, misspelt or using the wrong library address. Double check on your library names ( **case sensitive** such as ‚ÄúPRBMath‚Äù ) or ensure that a matching library name and library address is provided.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#missing-contract-name)

Missing Contract Name

‚ÄúUnable to locate ContractName , did you specify the correct Contract Name ?‚Äù

A match was not found with the name of the contract specified when multiple files are provided. Ensure that you have provided the correct contract name to be matched against, and making sure you submit the **main contract** name not its dependencies.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#missing/invalid-constructor-arguments)

Missing/Invalid Constructor Arguments

‚ÄúPlease check if the correct constructor argument was entered‚Äù

if your contract utilized the `constructor` keyword, you should provide it in hex format. Otherwise, leave this field empty as it is. You may reference your original deployment‚Äôs constructor arguments or determine it from the [**end of your compiled bytecode**](https://info.etherscan.com/contract-verification-constructor-arguments/)
.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#mismatched-bytecode-metadata-hash)

Mismatched bytecode metadata hash

‚ÄúPlease check if the correct bytecodehash was specified via standard-json verification.‚Äù

The [**metadata hash**](https://docs.soliditylang.org/en/v0.8.17/metadata.html#encoding-of-the-metadata-hash-in-the-bytecode)
 settings of your submitted source code differs from the settings of your original contract deployment, such as being set to `ipfs` or `none`. Submit your contract verification using the solc json input format, and [**specify the settings**](https://github.com/PaulRBerg/hardhat-template/blob/f6406c4e7c9e23d5169b39fb11d528a975b678e6/hardhat.config.ts#L104)
 accordingly there. Other submission formats such as single file or multifile **do not support** changing this setting, and will use the compiler defaults.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#similar-match-found)

Similar Match Found

‚ÄúThis contract already Similar Matches the deployed ByteCode at 0x4200000000000000000000000000000000000042‚Äù

This error indicates that the contract has already been verified via [**Similar Match**](https://info.etherscan.com/types-of-contract-verification/)
 to another contract. Kindly [**reach out**](https://info.etherscan.com/update-on-similar-match-contract-verification/)
 to us at this point of time to have this updated to Full Match if required.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#unsupported-solc-version)

Unsupported Solc Version

‚ÄúInvalid or not supported solc version, see [https://etherscan.io/solcversions](https://etherscan.io/solcversions)
 for list‚Äù

This error is thrown when you specify to use an invalid or unsupported version of the Solidity Compiler ie. below `v0.4.11-nightly.2017.3.15+`. Do [**let us know**](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/contact-us)
 if you need to verify a contract below this supported version such as to prove you deployed the first NFT.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#source-code-already-verified)

Source Code Already Verified

‚ÄúSource code already verified‚Äù

An [**Exact Match**](https://info.etherscan.com/types-of-contract-verification/)
 has been obtained, get back to having your [**coffee**](https://media.giphy.com/media/11ISwbgCxEzMyY/giphy.gif)
. If you think this might be a mistake, do check if you‚Äôve submitted verification to the right **explorer/chain**, a contract that is verified on Etherscan is **not automatically verified** on other explorers.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#unsupported-file-import-callback)

Unsupported File Import Callback

‚ÄúSource ‚Äú@openzeppelin/contracts/ERC20.sol‚Äù not found: File import callback not supported‚Äù

This error is thrown when contracts reference imports from external sources, such as [**OpenZeppelin**](https://docs.openzeppelin.com/)
 libraries or Github links. Consider [**flattening**](https://hardhat.org/hardhat-runner/docs/advanced/flattening#flattening-your-contracts)
 your source code into a single file, or use the Solidity Standard Json Input format that comes with tools such as [**Hardhat**](https://hardhat.org/hardhat-runner/docs/guides/verifying#verifying-your-contracts)
 to resolve these external imports.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/common-verification-errors#temporary-error)

Temporary Error

‚ÄúThis could be a temporary error, please retry or contact us (Error Code 10001/10002/10003)‚Äù

Something went wrong on our end, which could include downtime or [**maintenance**](https://etherscan.freshstatus.io/)
 windows. Please retry this in a while or [**ping us**](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/contact-us)
 if this continues to persist.

[Verify with Remix](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-remix)
[PRO Endpoints](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/pro-endpoints)

‚åòI

---

      "result": [\

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavghashrate#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavghashrate#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavghashrate#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavghashrate#param-module)

module

string

default:"stats"

Set to `stats` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavghashrate#param-action)

action

string

default:"dailyavghashrate"

Set to `dailyavghashrate` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavghashrate#param-startdate)

startdate

string

default:"2019-02-01"

Starting date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavghashrate#param-enddate)

enddate

string

default:"2019-02-28"

Ending date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavghashrate#param-sort)

sort

string

default:"desc"

Sort order either `desc` for the latest results first or `asc` for the oldest results first.

string

default:"dailynewaddress"

startdate

string

default:"2019-02-01"

enddate

string

default:"2019-02-28"

Ending date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailynewaddress#param-sort)

sort

string

default:"desc"

Sort order either `desc` for the latest results first or `asc` for the oldest results first.

.

string

integer

Ending block number to search to.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-topics#param-topic0)

topic0

string

First topic to filter by, such as an event signature.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-topics#param-topic0-1-opr)

topic0\_1\_opr

string

default:"and"

Topic operator between `topic0` and `topic1`, either `and` or `or`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-topics#param-topic1)

topic1

string

Second topic to filter by.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-topics#param-topic1-2-opr)

topic1\_2\_opr

string

default:"and"

Topic operator between `topic1` and `topic2`, either `and` or `or`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-topics#param-topic2)

topic2

string

Third topic to filter by.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-topics#param-topic2-3-opr)

topic2\_3\_opr

string

default:"and"

Topic operator between `topic2` and `topic3`, either `and` or `or`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-topics#param-topic3)

topic3

string

Fourth topic to filter by.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-topics#param-topic0-2-opr)

topic0\_2\_opr

string

default:"and"

Topic operator between `topic0` and `topic2`, either `and` or `or`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-topics#param-topic0-3-opr)

topic0\_3\_opr

string

default:"and"

Topic operator between `topic0` and `topic3`, either `and` or `or`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-topics#param-topic1-3-opr)

topic1\_3\_opr

string

default:"and"

Topic operator between `topic1` and `topic3`, either `and` or `or`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-topics#param-page)

page

integer

default:"1"

Page number for pagination.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-topics#param-offset)

offset

integer

default:"1000"

Number of records per page. Limited to 1000 records per query; use the `page` parameter for subsequent records.

# Verify with Foundry - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-foundry#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Contract Verification

Verify with Foundry

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

On this page

*   [Deploy and Verify](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-foundry#deploy-and-verify)
    
*   [Verify an Existing Contract](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-foundry#verify-an-existing-contract)
    
*   [Custom Chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-foundry#custom-chains)
    

Ensuring you‚Äôre using the latest version of Foundry, via `foundryup`

[**Foundry**](https://book.getfoundry.sh/)
 is a tool that helps take the heat off smart contract development steps, including compiling, deploying and finally submitting your contract for verification. This assumes you already have a [**Foundry project**](https://getfoundry.sh/guides/project-setup/creating-a-new-project)
**,** setup, and you‚Äôre about to deploy and verify next.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-foundry#deploy-and-verify)

Deploy and Verify
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    forge create --broadcast --rpc-url https://rpc.sepolia.ethpandaops.io --private-key YourPrivateKey src/ContractFile.sol:ContractName --verify --verifier etherscan --etherscan-api-key YourApiKeyToken
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-foundry#verify-an-existing-contract)

Verify an Existing Contract
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    forge verify-contract --watch --chain sepolia 0x324eca20b358b18e48f2611f7452560ce3b3c1bb src/ContractFile.sol:ContractName --verifier etherscan --etherscan-api-key YourApiKeyToken
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-foundry#custom-chains)

Custom Chains
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Most chains with an Etherscan explorer are supported using the `--chain` flag. For (very) new chains that aren‚Äôt natively supported by Foundry, you can use a custom `--verifier-url` Append the Etherscan V2 base path and the new chainId, in this example for Stable Testnet(2201).

Copy

Ask AI

    forge verify-contract 0x324eca20b358b18e48f2611f7452560ce3b3c1bb src/ContractFile.sol:ContractName --verifier etherscan --verifier-url "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=2201" --etherscan-api-key YourEtherscanApiKey --watch
    

> _This open source integration was shipped by_ [_@iainnash_](https://github.com/iainnash)
>  _and the Foundry team_

[Chainlist](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/chainlist)
[Verify with Hardhat](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat)

‚åòI

---

# Contact Us - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/contact-us#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Resources

Contact Us

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

On this page

*   [Support Tickets](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/contact-us#support-tickets)
    
*   [Twitter](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/contact-us#twitter)
    
*   [Freshstatus](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/contact-us#freshstatus)
    

Beware of **phishing attempts** and emails **impersonating the team** at Etherscan, we only communicate from the channels below.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/contact-us#support-tickets)

Support Tickets

Our emails always come from the domain **@etherscan.io**. Keep in mind that as a block explorer service, we **cannot cancel, refund or reverse transactions** as we do not process them. If your issues are related to transactions, you may find helpful articles over at the [**Etherscan Information Center.**](https://info.etherscan.com/)

Reach out to us via a [**support ticket.**](https://etherscan.io/contactus)

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/contact-us#twitter)

Twitter

For general updates, new feature releases and community support, keep in touch with us via Twitter.

Follow us on [**Twitter.**](https://twitter.com/etherscan)

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/contact-us#freshstatus)

Freshstatus

Announcements for ongoing and scheduled maintenance works that may affect certain services used.

Check Etherscan‚Äôs [**network status.**](https://etherscan.freshstatus.io/)

[Common Error Messages](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/common-error-messages)

‚åòI

# Get Daily Transaction Count - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailytx#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

Navigation

Stats

Get Daily Transaction Count

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

GET

/

v2

/

api

Try it

Copy

Ask AI

curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=stats&action=dailytx&startdate=2019-02-01&enddate=2019-02-28&sort=desc&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-01",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1548979200",\
          "transactionCount": 498856\
        },\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-02",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1549065600",\
          "transactionCount": 450314\
        }\
      ]
    }

This is a PRO endpoint, available to any [paid tier](https://etherscan.io/apis)

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailytx#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailytx#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailytx#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailytx#param-module)

module

string

default:"stats"

Set to `stats` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailytx#param-action)

action

string

default:"dailytx"

Set to `dailytx` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailytx#param-startdate)

startdate

string

default:"2019-02-01"

Starting date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailytx#param-enddate)

enddate

string

default:"2019-02-28"

Ending date in `yyyy-MM-dd` format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailytx#param-sort)

sort

string

default:"desc"

Sort order either `desc` for the latest results first or `asc` for the oldest results first.

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=stats&action=dailytx&startdate=2019-02-01&enddate=2019-02-28&sort=desc&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"
    

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-01",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1548979200",\
          "transactionCount": 498856\
        },\
        {\
          "UTCDate": "2019-02-02",\
          "unixTimeStamp": "1549065600",\
          "transactionCount": 450314\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

[Get Daily Average Network Hash Rate](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavghashrate)
[Get Daily Average Network Difficulty](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgnetdifficulty)

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getdeposittxs#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getdeposittxs#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getdeposittxs#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"10"

Chain ID to query, eg `10` for Optimism or `42161` for Arbitrum from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getdeposittxs#param-module)

module

string

default:"account"

Set to `account` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getdeposittxs#param-action)

action

string

default:"getdeposittxs"

Set to `getdeposittxs` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getdeposittxs#param-address)

address

string

default:"0x80f3950a4d371c43360f292a4170624abd9eed03"

Address to check for cross-chain deposits from Ethereum to L2.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getdeposittxs#param-page)

page

integer

default:"1"

Page number for pagination.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getdeposittxs#param-offset)

offset

integer

default:"10"

Number of records per page.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getdeposittxs#param-sort)

sort

string

default:"desc"

Sort order either `desc` for the latest transactions first or `asc` for the oldest transactions first.

Ask AI

    curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=10&module=account&action=getdeposittxs&address=0x80f3950a4d371c43360f292a4170624abd9eed03&page=1&offset=10&sort=desc&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"
