### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getblocknobytime#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getblocknobytime#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getblocknobytime#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID you query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getblocknobytime#param-module)

module

string

default:"block"

Set to `block` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getblocknobytime#param-action)

action

string

default:"getblocknobytime"

Set to `getblocknobytime` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getblocknobytime#param-timestamp)

timestamp

integer

default:"1578638524"

Unix timestamp in seconds.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getblocknobytime#param-closest)

closest

string

default:"before"

Closest available block to the provided timestamp, either `before` or `after`.

apikey

.

module

string

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-address-topics#param-action)

action

string

default:"getLogs"

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-address-topics#param-from-block)

fromBlock

integer

default:"15073139"

Starting block number to search from.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-address-topics#param-to-block)

toBlock

integer

default:"15074139"

Ending block number to search to.

address

string

default:"0x59728544b08ab483533076417fbbb2fd0b17ce3a"

Address to check for logs.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-address-topics#param-topic0)

topic0

string

First topic to filter by, such as an event signature.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-address-topics#param-topic0-1-opr)

topic0\_1\_opr

string

default:"and"

Topic operator between `topic0` and `topic1`, either `and` or `or`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-address-topics#param-topic1)

topic1

string

Second topic to filter by.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-address-topics#param-page)

page

integer

default:"1"

Page number for pagination.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getlogs-address-topics#param-offset)

offset

integer

default:"1000"

Number of records per page. Limited to 1000 records per query; use the `page` parameter for subsequent records.

# V2 Migration - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/v2-migration#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Get Started

V2 Migration

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

On this page

*   [How to Migrate](https://docs.etherscan.io/v2-migration#how-to-migrate)
    

[Contract verification](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-foundry)
 using Hardhat/Remix/Foundry also support using a single Etherscan API key for all chains

As of¬†**August 15th, 2025**, the legacy¬†**Etherscan API V1 endpoints have been deprecated**¬†in favor of the new¬†**Etherscan API V2**, which introduces a unified multichain experience across 60+ supported networks üåà. You‚Äôll see a deprecation error message like this if you‚Äôre still using V1:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
       "status":"0",
       "message":"NOTOK",
       "result":"You are using a deprecated V1 endpoint, switch to Etherscan API V2."
    }
    

All existing endpoints remain compatible once you update them to the¬†**V2 format**.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/v2-migration#how-to-migrate)

How to Migrate

1

Create an Etherscan account

[**Sign up**](https://etherscan.io/register)
 if you don‚Äôt have an account or if you‚Äôre using other explorers like BaseScan, BscScan, Polygonscan, etc.

2

Create an Etherscan API Key

Under your Etherscan [**API dashboard**](https://etherscan.io/apidashboard)
, create a new key. This key can be used to access all¬†[supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
¬†under API V2.

3

Migrating Endpoints from Etherscan API V1

Use¬†`https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api`¬†as your¬†**base path**, and include a¬†`chainid`¬†for your target network (e.g.,¬†1¬†for Ethereum).Before (V1):

Copy

Ask AI

    https://api.etherscan.io/api?&action=balance&apikey=YourEtherscanApiKey
    

After (V2):

Copy

Ask AI

    https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&action=balance&apikey=YourEtherscanApiKey
    

4

Migrating Endpoints from Other Explorers

Use the same base path (`https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api`) and include a `chainid` for the relevant chain from [this list](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
, in this case `137` for Polygon.Pass in your **Etherscan API key** instead of the old explorer-specific one.Before (PolygonScan V1):

Copy

Ask AI

    https://api.polygonscan.com/api?&action=balance&apikey=YourPolygonscanApiKey
    

After (V2):

Copy

Ask AI

    https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=137&action=balance&apikey=YourEtherscanApiKey
    

[Rate Limits](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/rate-limits)
[Get Native Balance for an Address](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balance)

‚åòI

---

Ask AI

    curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=stats&action=ethsupply2&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"
    

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": {
        "EthSupply": "122373866217800000000000000",
        "Eth2Staking": "2940327167090033000000000",
        "BurntFees": "4610942856337430575173814",
        "WithdrawnTotal": "7618584348954597000000000"
      }
    }

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Get Started

Getting an API Key

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

1

Create an Etherscan Account

[Sign up](https://etherscan.io/register)
 for a Free account.

2

Navigate to the API Dashboard

Under your [API Dashboard](https://etherscan.io/apidashboard)
, click ‚ÄúAdd +‚Äù to create a new API key. This key can be used to access all [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
 under API V2.![Remix verify](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/7r1uhEYn3uP2ppZz/images/dashboard-keys.avif?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=7r1uhEYn3uP2ppZz&q=85&s=74c627eca1162db3caa62a7324bf5861)

3

Make your First Request

Use your key to start testing requests in the [API Playground](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference)
 within this docs üöÄ.

[Introduction](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Supported Chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)

string

default:"2019-02-01"

string

default:"2019-02-28"

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethdailyprice#param-sort)

sort

string

default:"desc"

Sort order either `desc` for the latest results first or `asc` for the oldest results first.

# Verify with Hardhat - Etherscan

[Skip to main content](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat#content-area)

[Etherscan home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=de6b19ab2ee635186e20de82cb4684a0)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f/logo/etherscan-logo-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=3Bzz_zQxnltPim9f&q=85&s=637b866d48682d2277ff49a88ee1b61d)](https://docs.etherscan.io/)

Search...

‚åòK

Search...

Navigation

Contract Verification

Verify with Hardhat

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)
[Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.etherscan.io/mcp-docs/introduction)
[Metadata CSV](https://docs.etherscan.io/metadata/introduction)

On this page

*   [Install](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat#install)
    
*   [Config](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat#config)
    
*   [Deploy and Verify (using Hardhat Ignition)](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat#deploy-and-verify-using-hardhat-ignition)
    
*   [Verify an Existing Contract](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat#verify-an-existing-contract)
    
*   [Custom Chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat#custom-chains)
    

This guide covers Hardhat 3. There is an official [**migration guide**](https://hardhat.org/docs/hardhat3/migration)
 from the Hardhat team.

[**Hardhat**](https://hardhat.org/)
 is a smart contracts development tool, perfect if you‚Äôre familiar with Javascript/Typescript. This assumes you already have a [**Hardhat 3 project**](https://hardhat.org/docs/getting-started)
**,** setup, and you‚Äôre about to deploy and verify next.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat#install)

Install
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Via npm.

Copy

Ask AI

    npm add --save-dev @nomicfoundation/hardhat-verify
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat#config)

Config
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In `hardhat.config.ts`, import the plugin at the top and add it to the list of `plugins`. Then, specify a `verify` config with your Etherscan API key. This key works for most [**supported chains**](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
, otherwise you need to define a CustomChain below.

Copy

Ask AI

    import { defineConfig } from "hardhat/config";
    import hardhatVerify from "@nomicfoundation/hardhat-verify";
    
    export default defineConfig({
      plugins: [\
        hardhatVerify,\
        // ...other plugins...\
      ],
      solidity: "0.8.28",
      networks: {
        sepolia: {
          url: configVariable("SEPOLIA_RPC_URL"),
          accounts: [configVariable("SEPOLIA_PRIVATE_KEY")],
        },
      },
      verify: {
        etherscan: {
          apiKey: "YourEtherscanApiKey",
        },
      },
    });
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat#deploy-and-verify-using-hardhat-ignition)

Deploy and Verify (using Hardhat Ignition)
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    npx hardhat ignition deploy ignition/modules/Counter.ts --network sepolia --verify
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat#verify-an-existing-contract)

Verify an Existing Contract
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    npx hardhat verify --network sepolia 0xdCBdBAA8404554502B433106e62728B659aCfE3b
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-hardhat#custom-chains)

Custom Chains
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For new chains that have an Etherscan explorer but isn‚Äôt supported with Hardhat defaults, you need to add both the `networks` and `chainDescriptor` in `hardhat.config.ts`.

Copy

Ask AI

    export default defineConfig({
      // ...
      networks: {
        monadTestnet: {
          type: "http",
          chainType: "l1",
          url: configVariable("MONAD_TESTNET_RPC_URL"),
          accounts: [configVariable("MONAD_TESTNET_PRIVATE_KEY")],
        }
      },
      chainDescriptors: {
        10143: {
          name: "monadTestnet",
          blockExplorers: {
            etherscan: {
              name: "Monad Testnet Explorer",
              url: "https://testnet.monadscan.com",
              apiUrl: "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api",
            },
          },
        }
      },
    });
    

Use the same deploy and verify command as above, but with the updated `--network`. In this example for `monadTestnet`

Copy

Ask AI

    npx hardhat ignition deploy ignition/modules/Counter.ts --network monadTestnet --verify
    

[Verify with Foundry](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-foundry)
[Verify with Remix](https://docs.etherscan.io/contract-verification/verify-with-remix)

‚åòI

---

apikey

string

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethestimategas#param-data)

data

string

default:"0x4e71d92d"

Hash of the method signature and encoded parameters.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethestimategas#param-to)

to

string

default:"0xf0160428a8552ac9bb7e050d90eeade4ddd52843"

The address to interact with.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethestimategas#param-value)

value

string

default:"0xff22"

Value sent in this transaction, in hex.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethestimategas#param-gas-price)

gasPrice

string

default:"0x51da038cc"

Gas price in wei.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethestimategas#param-gas)

gas

string

default:"0x5f5e0ff"

Gas limit provided for the transaction, in hex.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgettransactionbyblocknumberandindex#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

apikey

string

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgettransactionbyblocknumberandindex#param-chainid)

string

.

default:"eth\_getTransactionByBlockNumberAndIndex"

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgettransactionbyblocknumberandindex#param-tag)

tag

string

default:"0xC6331D"

Block number in hex format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgettransactionbyblocknumberandindex#param-index)

index

string

default:"0x11A"

Transaction index position in the block, in hex.

Ask AI

    curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=proxy&action=eth_getTransactionByBlockNumberAndIndex&tag=0xC6331D&index=0x11A&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"

    {
      "jsonrpc": "2.0",
      "id": 1,

string

default:"getabi"

string

default:"0xBB9bc244D798123fDe783fCc1C72d3Bb8C189413"

string

.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgetunclebyblocknumberandindex#param-module)

module

string

default:"proxy"

Set to `proxy` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgetunclebyblocknumberandindex#param-action)

action

string

default:"eth\_getUncleByBlockNumberAndIndex"

Set to `eth_getUncleByBlockNumberAndIndex` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgetunclebyblocknumberandindex#param-tag)

tag

string

default:"0xC63276"

Block number in hex format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgetunclebyblocknumberandindex#param-index)

index

string

default:"0x0"

Position of the uncle in the block, in hex.

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgetblockbynumber#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgetblockbynumber#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgetblockbynumber#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgetblockbynumber#param-module)

module

string

default:"proxy"

Set to `proxy` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgetblockbynumber#param-action)

action

string

default:"eth\_getBlockByNumber"

Set to `eth_getBlockByNumber` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgetblockbynumber#param-tag)

tag

string

default:"0x10d4f"

Block number in hex format.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethgetblockbynumber#param-boolean)

boolean

string

default:"true"

Set to `true` to return full transaction objects or `false` for transaction hashes only.

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=proxy&action=eth_getBlockByNumber&tag=0x10d4f&boolean=true&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"

[API Documentation](https://docs.etherscan.io/introduction)

POST

/

api

Try it

Verify Proxy Contract

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.etherscan.io/api

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
        "status": "1",
        "message": "OK",
        "result": "a7lpxkm9kpcpicx7daftmjifrfhiuhf5vqqnawhkfhzfrcpnxj"
    }

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifyproxycontract#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifyproxycontract#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifyproxycontract#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifyproxycontract#param-module)

module

string

default:"contract"

Set to `contract` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifyproxycontract#param-action)

action

string

default:"verifyproxycontract"

Set to `verifyproxycontract` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifyproxycontract#param-address)

address

string

default:"0xcbdcd3815b5f975e1a2c944a9b2cd1c985a1cb7f"

The proxy contract address to verify.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifyproxycontract#param-expectedimplementation)

expectedimplementation

string

default:"0xB0F24CEB2616F6Bb608B00875Db306167c0f2E8C"

Optional implementation address to enforce during verification.

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
        "status": "1",
        "message": "OK",
        "result": "a7lpxkm9kpcpicx7daftmjifrfhiuhf5vqqnawhkfhzfrcpnxj"
    }

GET

/

v2

/

api

Try it

Copy

Ask AI

curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=token&action=tokenholdercount&contractaddress=0xaaaebe6fe48e54f431b0c390cfaf0b017d09d42d&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": "30506"
    }

This is a PRO endpoint, available to any [paid tier](https://etherscan.io/apis)

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenholdercount#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenholdercount#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenholdercount#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenholdercount#param-module)

module

string

default:"token"

Set to `token` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenholdercount#param-action)

action

string

default:"tokenholdercount"

Set to `tokenholdercount` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenholdercount#param-contractaddress)

contractaddress

string

default:"0xaaaebe6fe48e54f431b0c390cfaf0b017d09d42d"

Contract address of the ERC-20 token.

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=token&action=tokenholdercount&contractaddress=0xaaaebe6fe48e54f431b0c390cfaf0b017d09d42d&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"
    

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": "30506"
    }

v2

/

api

Try it

Copy

Ask AI

curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=account&action=tokenbalance&contractaddress=0x57d90b64a1a57749b0f932f1a3395792e12e7055&address=0xe04f27eb70e025b78871a2ad7eabe85e61212761&tag=latest&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"

Ask AI

{
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenbalance#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenbalance#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenbalance#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenbalance#param-module)

module

string

default:"account"

Set to `account` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenbalance#param-action)

action

string

default:"tokenbalance"

Set to `tokenbalance` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenbalance#param-contractaddress)

contractaddress

string

default:"0x57d90b64a1a57749b0f932f1a3395792e12e7055"

Contract address of the ERC-20 token.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenbalance#param-address)

address

string

default:"0xe04f27eb70e025b78871a2ad7eabe85e61212761"

Address to check for token balance.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenbalance#param-tag)

tag

string

default:"latest"

Use `latest` for the last block number of the chain.

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api?chainid=1&module=account&action=tokenbalance&contractaddress=0x57d90b64a1a57749b0f932f1a3395792e12e7055&address=0xe04f27eb70e025b78871a2ad7eabe85e61212761&tag=latest&apikey=YourApiKeyToken"
    

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": "135499"
    }

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getsourcecode#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getsourcecode#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getsourcecode#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getsourcecode#param-module)

module

string

default:"contract"

Set to `contract` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getsourcecode#param-action)

action

string

default:"getsourcecode"

Set to `getsourcecode` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getsourcecode#param-address)

address

string

default:"0xBB9bc244D798123fDe783fCc1C72d3Bb8C189413"

The contract address to query.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-module)

module

string

default:"contract"

Set to `contract` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-action)

action

string

default:"verifysourcecode"

Set to `verifysourcecode` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-contractaddress)

contractaddress

string

default:"0xBB9bc244D798123fDe783fCc1C72d3Bb8C189413"

The address where the contract is deployed.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-source-code)

sourceCode

string

The Solidity source code to verify.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-codeformat)

codeformat

string

default:"solidity-standard-json-input"

Use `solidity-single-file` for a single file or `solidity-standard-json-input` for JSON input.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-contractname)

contractname

string

default:"contracts/Verified.sol:Verified"

The contract name, including path if applicable. If `codeformat=solidity-standard-json-input`, then enter contractname as `erc20.sol:erc20`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-compilerversion)

compilerversion

string

default:"v0.8.24+commit.e11b9ed9"

Compiler version used for compilation.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-optimization-used)

optimizationUsed

string

default:"0"

Use `1` if optimization was used or `0` if disabled, specify runs below.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-runs)

runs

string

default:"200"

Number of optimization runs.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-constructor-arguments)

constructorArguments

string

Optional constructor arguments used in contract deployment.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-evm-version)

evmVersion

string

default:"default"

Use compiler `default` or specify an EVM version such as `byzantium`, `shanghai`.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifysourcecode#param-license-type)

licenseType

string

default:"1"

The [open source license](https://etherscan.io/contract-license-types)
 to associate with the verified source code, e.g `3` for MIT.

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
        "status": "1",
        "message": "OK",
        "result": "a7lpxkm9kpcpicx7daftmjifrfhiuhf5vqqnawhkfhzfrcpnxj"
    }
    

[Get Contract Creator and Creation Tx Hash](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/getcontractcreation)
[Verify Source Code on zkSync](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/verifyzksyncsourcecode)

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/token1155tx#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/token1155tx#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/token1155tx#param-module)

module

string

default:"account"

Set to `account` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/token1155tx#param-action)

action

string

default:"token1155tx"

Set to `token1155tx` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/token1155tx#param-contractaddress)

contractaddress

string

default:"0x76be3b62873462d2142405439777e971754e8e77"

The ERC1155 token contract address to filter transfers by, eg `0x495f947276749ce646f68ac8c248420045cb7b5e` for [Opensea Shared Storefront](https://etherscan.io/token/0x495f947276749ce646f68ac8c248420045cb7b5e)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/token1155tx#param-address)

address

string

default:"0x83f564d180b58ad9a02a449105568189ee7de8cb"

The address to query, like `0xfefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefefe`

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/token1155tx#param-page)

page

integer

default:"1"

Page number for pagination.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/token1155tx#param-offset)

offset

integer

default:"1"

Number of transactions per page.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/token1155tx#param-startblock)

startblock

integer

default:"0"

Starting block number to search from.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/token1155tx#param-endblock)

endblock

integer

default:"9999999999"

Ending block number to search to.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/token1155tx#param-sort)

sort

string

default:"desc"

Sort order either `desc` for the latest transactions first or `asc` for the oldest transactions first.

/

v2

/

api

Try it

Get Internal Transactions by Transaction Hash

cURL

Copy

Ask AI

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.etherscan.io/v2/api

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "blockNumber": "1743059",\
          "timeStamp": "1466489498",\
          "from": "0x2cac6e4b11d6b58f6d3c1c9d5fe8faa89f60e5a2",\
          "to": "0x66a1c3eaf0f1ffc28d209c0763ed0ca614f3b002",\
          "value": "7106740000000000",\
          "contractAddress": "",\
          "input": "",\
          "type": "call",\
          "gas": "2300",\
          "gasUsed": "0",\
          "isError": "0",\
          "errCode": ""\
        }\
      ]
    }

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/txlistinternal-txhash#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/txlistinternal-txhash#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/txlistinternal-txhash#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/txlistinternal-txhash#param-module)

module

string

default:"account"

Set to `account` for this endpoint

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/txlistinternal-txhash#param-action)

action

string

default:"txlistinternal"

Set to `txlistinternal` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/txlistinternal-txhash#param-txhash)

txhash

string

Transaction hash to check for internal transactions, like `0x36dc7f05085d0e4f9c3e4116345a2a487ac8f23f7e71bcc0ae20e27abbfa931d`. Only non-zero value internal transactions are returned.

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "blockNumber": "1743059",\
          "timeStamp": "1466489498",\
          "from": "0x2cac6e4b11d6b58f6d3c1c9d5fe8faa89f60e5a2",\
          "to": "0x66a1c3eaf0f1ffc28d209c0763ed0ca614f3b002",\
          "value": "7106740000000000",\
          "contractAddress": "",\
          "input": "",\
          "type": "call",\
          "gas": "2300",\
          "gasUsed": "0",\
          "isError": "0",\
          "errCode": ""\
        }\
      ]
    }

      "status": "1",

          "blockNumber": "4708120",\

          "blockHash": "0x4be19c278bfaead5cb0bc9476fa632e2447f6e6259e0303af210302d22779a24",\

          "contractAddress": "0x06012c8cf97bead5deae237070f9587f8e7a266d",\
          "to": "0x6975be450864c02b4613023c2152ee0743572325",\

          "tokenName": "CryptoKitties",\
          "tokenSymbol": "CK",\

          "confirmations": "18759540"\
        }\
      ]
    }

### 

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokennfttx#query-parameters)

Query Parameters

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokennfttx#param-apikey)

apikey

string

default:"YourApiKeyToken"

Your Etherscan API key.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokennfttx#param-chainid)

chainid

string

default:"1"

Chain ID to query, eg `1` for Ethereum, `8453` for Base from our [supported chains](https://docs.etherscan.io/supported-chains)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokennfttx#param-module)

module

string

default:"account"

Set to `account` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokennfttx#param-action)

action

string

default:"tokennfttx"

Set to `tokennfttx` for this endpoint.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokennfttx#param-contractaddress)

contractaddress

string

default:"0x06012c8cf97bead5deae237070f9587f8e7a266d"

The ERC721 token contract address to filter transfers by, eg `0xbd3531da5cf5857e7cfaa92426877b022e612cf8` for [Pudgy Penguins](https://etherscan.io/token/0xbd3531da5cf5857e7cfaa92426877b022e612cf8)
.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokennfttx#param-address)

address

string

default:"0x6975be450864c02b4613023c2152ee0743572325"

Address to filter token transfers by.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokennfttx#param-page)

page

integer

default:"1"

Page number for pagination.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokennfttx#param-offset)

offset

integer

default:"1"

Number of transactions per page.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokennfttx#param-startblock)

startblock

integer

default:"0"

Starting block number to search from.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokennfttx#param-endblock)

endblock

integer

default:"9999999999"

Ending block number to search to.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokennfttx#param-sort)

sort

string

default:"desc"

Sort order either `desc` for the latest transactions first or `asc` for the oldest transactions first.

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "blockNumber": "4708120",\
          "timeStamp": "1512907118",\
          "hash": "0x031e6968a8de362e4328d60dcc7f72f0d6fc84284c452f63176632177146de66",\
          "nonce": "0",\
          "blockHash": "0x4be19c278bfaead5cb0bc9476fa632e2447f6e6259e0303af210302d22779a24",\
          "from": "0xb1690c08e213a35ed9bab7b318de14420fb57d8c",\
          "contractAddress": "0x06012c8cf97bead5deae237070f9587f8e7a266d",\
          "to": "0x6975be450864c02b4613023c2152ee0743572325",\
          "tokenID": "202106",\
          "tokenName": "CryptoKitties",\
          "tokenSymbol": "CK",\
          "tokenDecimal": "0",\
          "transactionIndex": "81",\
          "gas": "158820",\

      "status": "1",

        {\
          "TokenHolderAddress": "0x4da27a545c0c5b758a6ba100e3a049001de870f5",\

        },\
        {\
          "TokenHolderAddress": "0xa700b4eb416be35b2911fd5dee80678ff64ff6c9",\

          "TokenHolderAddressType": "C"\
        }\
      ]
    }

This is a PRO endpoint, available to any [paid tier](https://etherscan.io/apis)

This [historical endpoint](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/rate-limits)
 is throttled to 2 calls/s

HyperEVM (999) is not supported yet

![Token holders](https://mintcdn.com/etherscan/_gIsWVKPgcVhiZQW/images/features/holders.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=_gIsWVKPgcVhiZQW&q=85&s=10569f23cde4d2374743a40c7f6fc00d)

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/txsbeaconwithdrawal#query-parameters)

integer

default:"1"

Number of records per page.

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/txsbeaconwithdrawal#param-sort)

sort

string

default:"desc"

Sort order either `desc` for the latest transactions first or `asc` for the oldest transactions first.

Response

Copy

Ask AI

      "status": "1",
      "message": "OK",
      "result": [\
        {\
          "withdrawalIndex": "13",\
          "validatorIndex": "117823",\

          "amount": "3402931175",\
          "blockNumber": "17034877",\
          "timestamp": "1681338599"\

      ]
    }

Account
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Get Historical Native Balance for an Address](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/balancehistory)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/pro-endpoints#tokens)

Tokens
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Get Historical ERC20-Token Account Balance by BlockNo](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenbalancehistory)
    
*   [Get Historical ERC20-Token TotalSupply by ContractAddress & BlockNo](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokensupplyhistory)
    
*   [Get Top Token Holders](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/toptokenholders)
    
*   [Get Token Holder List by Contract Address](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenholderlist)
    
*   [Get Token Holder Count by Contract Address](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/tokenholdercount)
    
*   [Get Address ERC20 Token Holding](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokenbalance)
    
*   [Get Address ERC721 Token Holding](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftbalance)
    
*   [Get Address ERC721 Token Inventory by Contract](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/addresstokennftinventory)
    

[‚Äã](https://docs.etherscan.io/resources/pro-endpoints#blocks)

Blocks
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Get Daily Average Block Size](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgblocksize)
    
*   [Get Daily Block Count and Rewards](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyblkcount)
    
*   [Get Daily Block Rewards](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyblockrewards)
    
*   [Get Daily Average Block Time](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgblocktime)
    
*   [Get Daily Uncle Block Count and Rewards](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyuncleblkcount)

*   [Get Daily Network Utilization](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailynetutilization)
    
*   [Get Daily Average Network Hash Rate](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavghashrate)
    
*   [Get Daily Transaction Count](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailytx)
    
*   [Get Daily Average Network Difficulty](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/dailyavgnetdifficulty)
    
*   [Get Ether Historical Price](https://docs.etherscan.io/api-reference/endpoint/ethdailyprice)
